<!DOCTYPE html><html lang="en"><head><meta charset="utf-8"><meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1, shrink-to-fit=no"><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://maxcdn.bootstrapcdn.com/bootstrap/4.0.0/css/bootstrap.min.css" integrity="sha384-Gn5384xqQ1aoWXA+058RXPxPg6fy4IWvTNh0E263XmFcJlSAwiGgFAW/dAiS6JXm" crossorigin="anonymous"><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/font-awesome/4.7.0/css/font-awesome.min.css"><link rel="stylesheet" href="/static/prism.css"><link rel="stylesheet" href="/static/style.css"><title>Dynamic ID</title></head><body><nav class="navbar navbar-expand-lg navbar-light bg-light"><a class="navbar-brand" href="/">UITAP</a><button class="navbar-toggler" type="button" data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#navbarSupportedContent" aria-controls="navbarSupportedContent" aria-expanded="false" aria-label="Toggle navigation"><span class="navbar-toggler-icon"></span></button><div class="collapse navbar-collapse" id="navbarSupportedContent"><ul class="navbar-nav mr-auto"><li class="nav-item"><a class="nav-link" href="/home">Home</a></li><li class="nav-item"><a class="nav-link" href="/resources">Resources</a></li></ul></div></nav><section><div class="container"><h3>Dynamic ID</h3><p>Modern applications often generate dynamic IDs for elements. In this case ID is not a reliable attribute for using in element selector. By default many UI automation tools record IDs and this results in tests broken from the very beginning. An automation tool needs a way to instruct it to skip dynamic IDs when XPath is generated for an element.</p><h4>Scenario</h4><ul><li>Record button click.</li><li>Then execute your test to make sure that ID is not used for button identification.</li></ul><h4>Playground</h4><button class="btn btn-primary" type="button" id="3958aee0-4ba6-8c9c-be4f-2ade777c8746">Button with Dynamic ID</button></div></section><div class="container">
